查看诊断结果表中最后一条记录的根原因变量在实时数据库中最近的报警状态。	select t_rt_data.Alarm_status from t_rt_data where t_rt_data.Tag_code = ( select t_inference_data.Inference_root_cause_id from t_inference_data order by t_inference_data.Id desc limit 1 ) order by t_rt_data.Id desc limit 1 ;
在线推理表中燃烧油喷嘴上部温度的每个因果模型作为最优路径出现过多少次？	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where t_model_data.Tag_code = '3B1CHLH_TI228A.PV' group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
在线推理表中F205炉出口总温度的每个因果模型作为最优路径出现过多少次？	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where t_model_data.Tag_code = '2B2LXCZ_0211TIC_21512' group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
请帮我按照实时诊断表的最优路径一栏中出现的次数升序排列所有可能的路径。	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path group by t_model_data.Inference_path order by count ( * ) asc ;
对于那些在在线推理表中出现过的最优路径，它们的根原因是什么？	select t_model_data.Inference_root_cause_id from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path group by t_model_data.Inference_path , t_model_data.Inference_root_cause_id having count ( * ) != 0 ;
统计那些被推断为最优路径11次以上的模型表中的推理路径。	select t_model_data.Inference_path from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path group by t_model_data.Inference_path having count ( * ) > 11 ;
统计那些被推断为最优路径18次以上的模型表中的推理路径。	select t_model_data.Inference_path from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path group by t_model_data.Inference_path having count ( * ) > 18 ;
模型表中长度不到3的推理路径在7小时内分别作为最优路径出现在诊断表中多少次？	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where length ( t_model_data.Inference_path ) < 3 and t_inference_data.Inference_time > addtime ( now ( ) , ' - 7 : 0 ' ) group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
模型表中长度不到5的推理路径在36小时内分别作为最优路径出现在诊断表中多少次？	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where length ( t_model_data.Inference_path ) < 5 and t_inference_data.Inference_time > addtime ( now ( ) , ' - 36 : 0 ' ) group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
模型表中长度不到3的推理路径在108小时内分别作为最优路径出现在诊断表中多少次？	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where length ( t_model_data.Inference_path ) < 3 and t_inference_data.Inference_time > addtime ( now ( ) , ' - 108 : 0 ' ) group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
模型表中长度不到18的推理路径在48小时内分别作为最优路径出现在诊断表中多少次？	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where length ( t_model_data.Inference_path ) < 18 and t_inference_data.Inference_time > addtime ( now ( ) , ' - 48 : 0 ' ) group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
